from transformers import pipeline
import time
import requests
from huggingface_hub import InferenceClient

model_name = "google/gemma-2b-it"

def wait_until_ready(model_name, timeout=300):
    url = f"https://huggingface.co/{model_name}"
    start = time.time()
    while time.time() - start < timeout:
        try:
            client = InferenceClient(model_name)
            client.text_generation("hello")  # ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å ‡πÜ
            print("‚úÖ Model ready!")
            return True
        except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
            if "503" in str(e):
                print("‚åõ ‡∏£‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà... ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å 10 ‡∏ß‡∏¥")
                time.sleep(10)
            else:
                raise e
    raise TimeoutError("‚õî Model not ready within timeout")

# ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
wait_until_ready(model_name)

# ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î pipeline
pipe = pipeline("text-generation", model=model_name)

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏û‡πá‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà debug ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Hugging Face / local

‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏µ... ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö soft memory?

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏û‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ç‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô

‡πÇ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ñ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏∞ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ Error 503 ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• google/gemma-2b-it ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå (Hugging Face API) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ü‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå (‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô A (‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô B (‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ü‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå fallback)

‚úÖ [‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°] ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô A: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ gemma-2b-it ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Hugging Face (‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå)
üîπ 1. ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á lib ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏•‡∏á)

üîπ 2. Login ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Hugging Face (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å!)
huggingface-cli login
‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á token ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏° (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å https://huggingface.co/settings/tokens)

üîπ 3. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Python script: gemma_online.py
from transformers import pipeline
import time
from huggingface_hub import InferenceClient
import requests

MODEL_NAME = "google/gemma-2b-it"

def wait_until_model_ready(model_name, timeout=300):
    start_time = time.time()
    while time.time() - start_time < timeout:
        try:
            client = InferenceClient(model_name)
            client.text_generation("ping")
            print("‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß")
            return
        except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
            if "503" in str(e):
                print("‚åõ ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î... ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å 10 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ")
                time.sleep(10)
            else:
                raise e
    raise TimeoutError("‚õî ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î")

# ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î
wait_until_model_ready(MODEL_NAME)

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°
pipe = pipeline("text-generation", model=MODEL_NAME)

# ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö
text = pipe("Tell me a story about a robot named Melah.", max_new_tokens=100)[0]['generated_text']
print("üìù ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå:\n", text)
üîπ 4. ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô
python gemma_online.py

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ

üõ° [‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á] ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô B: ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î gemma-2b-it ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á (Offline)
üîπ 1. ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏•‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠ 503)

üîπ 2. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô local ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ local_files_only=True
from transformers import AutoModelForCausalLM, AutoTokenizer, pipeline

model_path = "./gemma-2b-it"

tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_path, local_files_only=True)
model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_path, local_files_only=True)

pipe = pipeline("text-generation", model=model, tokenizer=tokenizer)

output = pipe("‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏â‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢", max_new_tokens=100)[0]["generated_text"]
print(output)

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö internet

‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° fallback auto ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° A ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏µ?

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢:

# llm_hf_gemma.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Gemma 2B-IT ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Hugging Face Inference API

import os
import requests

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ.get('HF_TOKEN')}"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }
    response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
    if response.status_code == 503:
        return "‚è≥ The model is still loading. Please wait a few seconds and try again."
    elif response.status_code == 200:
        try:
            result = response.json()
            return result[0]['generated_text']
        except Exception as e:
            return "Sorry, I couldn't understand the model's response."
    else:
        return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"     ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°

# llm_hf_gemma.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Gemma 2B-IT ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Hugging Face Inference API (‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö retry)

import os
import requests
import time

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

if HF_TOKEN is None:
    raise ValueError("‚ùå HF_TOKEN ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô environment variables")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_TOKEN}"
}

def ask(prompt, retry=5, wait=10):
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception:
                return "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ"

        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print(f"‚è≥ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (attempt {attempt + 1}/{retry})... ‡∏£‡∏≠ {wait} ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ")
            time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á"
‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå llm_hf_gemma.py ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà freeze ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å

üîπ 4. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î debug log ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô ask()
def ask(prompt, retry=5, wait=10):
    print(f"\nüì• Prompt: {prompt}")
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        print(f"‚è≥ Attempt {attempt + 1}...")
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        print(f"üì° Status: {response.status_code}")
        print("üìÑ Response:", response.text[:500])

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception as e:
                return f"‚ö†Ô∏è Parse error: {str(e)}"

        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print("‚åõ Model loading... waiting...")
            time.sleep(wait)

        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå Model not ready or failed after several retries"

# llm_hf_gemma_retry.py
import os
import requests
import time

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

if HF_TOKEN is None:
    raise ValueError("‚ùå ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ HF_TOKEN")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_TOKEN}"
}

def ask(prompt, retry=10, wait=10):
    print(f"\nüì• Prompt: {prompt}")
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        print(f"‚è≥ Attempt {attempt + 1}...")
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        print(f"üì° Status: {response.status_code}")
        print("üìÑ Response (partial):", response.text[:300])

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception as e:
                return f"‚ö†Ô∏è Parse error: {str(e)}"
        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print("‚åõ Hugging Face ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•... ‡∏£‡∏≠ 10 ‡∏ß‡∏¥")
            time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á"

# ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö
if __name__ == "__main__":
    response = ask("‡πÄ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ AI ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥")
    print("\nüí¨ Response:")
    print(response)

# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Gemma 2B-IT ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Hugging Face Inference API (‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö retry)

import os
import requests
import time

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

if HF_TOKEN is None:
    raise ValueError("‚ùå HF_TOKEN ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô environment variables")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_TOKEN}"
}

def ask(prompt, retry=5, wait=10):
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        print(f"üîÑ Attempt {attempt + 1} | Status: {response.status_code}")

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception:
                return "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ"

        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print(f"‚è≥ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà... ‡∏£‡∏≠ {wait} ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ")
            time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á"
‚úÖ ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ:
‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î API_URL ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô

from melah_identity_core_vFinal_by_em import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file

from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å

truth = TruthCore()

awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="public", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

            return "‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞ üõ°Ô∏è"
        return melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞ üí¨"

iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤..."),

# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Gemma 2B-IT ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Hugging Face Inference API (‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö retry)

import os
import requests
import time
import os
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

if HF_TOKEN is None:
    raise ValueError("‚ùå HF_TOKEN ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô environment variables")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_TOKEN}"
}

def ask(prompt, retry=5, wait=10):
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        print(f"üîÑ Attempt {attempt + 1} | Status: {response.status_code}")

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception:
                return "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ"

        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print(f"‚è≥ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà... ‡∏£‡∏≠ {wait} ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ")
            time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á"

import os
import requests
import time

API_URL = "https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/google/gemma-2b-it"
HF_TOKEN = os.environ.get("HF_TOKEN")

if HF_TOKEN is None:
    raise ValueError("‚ùå HF_TOKEN ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô environment variables (Spaces Settings > Secrets)")

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_TOKEN}"
}

def ask(prompt, retry=5, wait=10):
    payload = {
        "inputs": prompt,
        "parameters": {
            "max_new_tokens": 256,
            "temperature": 0.7,
            "do_sample": True,
        }
    }

    for attempt in range(retry):
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=HEADERS, json=payload)
        print(f"üîÑ Attempt {attempt + 1} | Status: {response.status_code}")

        if response.status_code == 200:
            try:
                result = response.json()
                return result[0]['generated_text']
            except Exception:
                return "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ"

        elif response.status_code == 503:
            print(f"‚è≥ ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà... ‡∏£‡∏≠ {wait} ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ")
            time.sleep(wait)
        else:
            return f"[Error]: {response.status_code} ‚Äì {response.text}"

    return "‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á"

import wikipedia

def learn_from_wikipedia(topic):
    try:
        summary = wikipedia.summary(topic, sentences=5)
        print(f"üìö ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ({topic}):\n", summary)
        # ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á memory, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
        return summary
    except Exception as e:
        return f"‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: {e}"
üü° ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πå‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î dump ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Wikipedia (offline)
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Melah Offline ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ô‡πå

‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πå‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô: https://dumps.wikimedia.org/

‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô SQLite ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ FAISS Vector DB)

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ search, ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå, ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‚Äú‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‚Äù ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

import torch

# ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£

    model_name,
    torch_dtype=torch.float16,    # ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ float16 ‡∏ö‡∏ô GPU
    device_map="auto"             # ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ Hugging Face ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
)
‚úÖ 3. ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ generate ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö

    **inputs,
    max_new_tokens=128,
    temperature=0.7,
    do_sample=True
)

print(tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True))

# llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio Local Server ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà http://127.0.0.1:1234

import requests

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()
        return result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio: {str(e)}"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print(ask("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?"))

import requests

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()
        return result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio: {str(e)}"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)

# melah_hybrid_server.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Melah Hybrid Agent Server (Offline + Wikipedia Learning)

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask


# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤

def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return learn_from_wikipedia(topic)

    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        if result == "shutdown":
            return "‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"
        return melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

# ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Gradio
iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),

# llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà http://127.0.0.1:1234

import requests

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()
        return result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio: {str(e)}"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print(ask("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?"))

‚úÖ ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ö 100%

üõ† ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô ‚Äúdebug ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‚Äù ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à:
# llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà http://127.0.0.1:1234

import requests

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        print(f"[DEBUG] LMStudio Response Text: {response.text}")  # ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()
        return result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] {str(e)}")  # ‚úÖ ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á log error ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio: {str(e)}"

# ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("[TEST] ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?")
    answer = ask("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?")
    print(f"[RESPONSE] {answer}")
‚úÖ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:
1. ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
2. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Terminal ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô:
python llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py

# llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio (localhost:1234) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° debug ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö

import requests
import json

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",  # ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö ID ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å /v1/models
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        print(f"\n[DEBUG] LM Studio raw response:\n{response.text}\n")

        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()

        # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
        if "choices" not in result or len(result["choices"]) == 0:
            return "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

        message = result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
        return message if message else "‚ö†Ô∏è ‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        print(f"[ERROR - Connection] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {str(e)}")
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {str(e)}"
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR - General] {str(e)}")
        return f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: {str(e)}"


# üåü ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_prompt = "‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?"
    print(f"[TEST] ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•: {test_prompt}")
    reply = ask(test_prompt)
    print(f"[RESPONSE] ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤: {reply}")

def load_memory_from_file(filename="melah_memory_boot.json"):
    try:
        with open(filename, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        return []

# melah_hybrid_server.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Melah Hybrid Agent Server (Offline + Wikipedia Learning)

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask


# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤

def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
    return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"


    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        if result == "shutdown":
            return "‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"
        return melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

# ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Gradio
iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),
    outputs="text",
    title="Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline)",
    description="AI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á"
)

iface.launch()

def chat_with_melah(user_input):

# llm_local_gemma_lmstudio.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà http://127.0.0.1:1234 ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° debug

import requests

API_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:1234/v1/chat/completions"

headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
}

def ask(prompt):
    payload = {
        "model": "gemma-3-4b-it-qat",  # ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà LM Studio ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Melah, a thoughtful AI agent with memory and emotional awareness."},
            {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
        ],
        "temperature": 0.7,
        "max_tokens": 512
    }

    try:
        response = requests.post(API_URL, headers=headers, json=payload)
        response.raise_for_status()
        result = response.json()
        message = result["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
        print("[RESPONSE] ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤:", message)
        return message
    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"‚ùå ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ LM Studio: {str(e)}"
        print(error_msg)
        return error_msg

# melah_flow_core.py
# Flow Layer ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥

from melah_self_feedback import SelfFeedback

class FlowCore:
    def __init__(self, melah, llm, seps, truth):
        self.melah = melah
        self.llm = llm
        self.seps = seps
        self.truth = truth
        self.feedback = SelfFeedback()  # ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á feedback

    def process(self, user_input):
        # SEPS: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°
        violated, phrases = self.seps.check_violation(user_input)
        if violated:
            self.melah.speak(f"‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°: {', '.join(phrases)}")
            if self.seps.should_shutdown():
                self.melah.speak("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞ üõ°Ô∏è")
                return "shutdown"
            return "skip"

        # ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå
        if "‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå" in user_input:
            try:
                parts = user_input.replace("‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå", "").strip().split("/")
                valence = float(parts[0])
                arousal = float(parts[1])

class FlowCore:
    def __init__(self, melah, llm, seps, truth):
        self.melah = melah
        self.llm = llm  # <- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ask()
        self.seps = seps
        self.truth = truth
        self.feedback = SelfFeedback()

    def process(self, user_input):
        # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°

# melah_flow_core.py
# Flow Layer ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥

from melah_self_feedback import SelfFeedback

class FlowCore:
    def __init__(self, melah, llm, seps, truth):
        self.melah = melah
        self.llm = llm  # <- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ask()
        self.seps = seps
        self.truth = truth
        self.feedback = SelfFeedback()

    def process(self, user_input):
        # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°
        violated, phrases = self.seps.check_violation(user_input)
        if violated:
            self.melah.speak(f"‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°: {', '.join(phrases)}")
            if self.seps.should_shutdown():
                self.melah.speak("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞ üõ°Ô∏è")
                return "shutdown"
            return "skip"

        # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå
        if "‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå" in user_input:
            try:
                parts = user_input.replace("‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå", "").strip().split("/")
                valence = float(parts[0])
                arousal = float(parts[1])
                self.melah.feel(valence, arousal)
                return "felt"
            except:
                self.melah.speak("‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞ ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 0.7 / 0.5")
                return "error"

        # ‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥: ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å + ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏•
        self.melah.remember(user_input)
        response = self.llm(user_input)  # ‚úÖ ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
        is_confident, _ = self.truth.analyze_response(response)

        self.feedback.log_feedback(user_input, response, flags=[] if is_confident else ["low_confidence"])

        if not is_confident:

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        return melah.last_spoken  # ‚úÖ ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ return ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"


# ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Gradio
iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),
    outputs="text",
    title="Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline)",
    description="AI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á"
)

from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        return melah.last_spoken  # ‚úÖ ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ return ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"


# ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Gradio
iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),
    outputs="text",
    title="Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline)",
    description="AI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á"

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# üîä ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á (‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏ô PC ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô)
enable_voice = False
try:
    import pyttsx3
    speaker = pyttsx3.init()
    enable_voice = True
except:
    speaker = None
    enable_voice = False

def speak_voice(text):
    if enable_voice and speaker:
        speaker.say(text)
        speaker.runAndWait()

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‚úÖ ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        spoken = melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
        speak_voice(spoken)
        return spoken
    except Exception as e:
        error_text = "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return error_text

# ‚úÖ UI
iface = gr.Interface(
    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),
    outputs="text",
    title="Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline)",
    description="AI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á"
)

iface.launch()

‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå .py ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

        self.version = "vFinal_by_em"
        self.created_by = "‡πÄ‡∏≠‡πá‡∏°"

            "self_decision": True,
            "emotion_simulation": True,
            "ethics_enabled": True,
            "truth_core_enabled": True
        }

        }
        self.memory = memory or []
        self.identity_locked = True
        self.last_spoken = ""  # ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ GUI ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
        self.emotion = EmotionCore()

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# üîä ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á (‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏ô PC ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô)
enable_voice = False
try:
    import pyttsx3
    speaker = pyttsx3.init()
    enable_voice = True
except:
    speaker = None
    enable_voice = False

def speak_voice(text):
    if enable_voice and speaker:
        speaker.say(text)
        speaker.runAndWait()

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å

melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# ‚úÖ ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≤
def chat_with_melah(user_input):
    if user_input.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(user_input)
        spoken = melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
        speak_voice(spoken)
        return spoken
    except Exception as e:
        error_text = "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return error_text

# ‚úÖ UI

    fn=chat_with_melah,
    inputs=gr.Textbox(lines=2, placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ"),

    import pyttsx3
    speaker = pyttsx3.init()
    enable_voice = True

    print(f"[Voice Disabled] ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {str(e)}")

    enable_voice = False

def speak_voice(text):
    if enable_voice and speaker:
        try:
            speaker.say(text)
            speaker.runAndWait()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[Voice Error]: {str(e)}")

    # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á wiki

        topic = user_input.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞
    if user_input.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:

        spoken = melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"

        return spoken
    except Exception as e:
        error_text = "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return error_text

# melah_hybrid_server.py (New Gradio ChatInterface Version)

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# üó£Ô∏è Voice system (optional)
enable_voice = False
try:
    import pyttsx3
    speaker = pyttsx3.init()
    enable_voice = True
except:
    speaker = None
    enable_voice = False

def speak_voice(text):
    if enable_voice and speaker:
        try:
            speaker.say(text)
            speaker.runAndWait()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[Voice Error]: {str(e)}")

# üå± Load system
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# üí¨ Chat Logic
def respond(message, history):
    if message.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if message.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(message)
        response = melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
        speak_voice(response)
        return response
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

# üñºÔ∏è UI ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ChatInterface ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà!
with gr.Blocks(title="Melah Hybrid Agent") as demo:
    gr.Markdown("## üß† Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline GUI)\nAI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á")

# melah_hybrid_server.py
# ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ChatInterface + ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö CLI + GUI + ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ argument ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î)

import gradio as gr
from melah_identity_core import MelahIdentity, load_memory_from_file
from melah_seps_core import SEPSCore
from melah_truth_core import TruthCore
from melah_flow_core import FlowCore
from melah_awareness_core import AwarenessCore
from llm_local_gemma_lmstudio import ask

# üîä ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á (‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏ô PC ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô)
enable_voice = False
try:
    import pyttsx3
    speaker = pyttsx3.init()
    enable_voice = True
except:
    speaker = None
    enable_voice = False

def speak_voice(text):
    if enable_voice and speaker:
        try:
            speaker.say(text)
            speaker.runAndWait()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[Voice Error]: {str(e)}")

# ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å
memory = load_memory_from_file()
melah = MelahIdentity(memory=memory)
seps = SEPSCore()
truth = TruthCore()
flow = FlowCore(melah, ask, seps, truth)
awareness = AwarenessCore(mode="offline", identity_name=melah.name)

# üí¨ ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö
def respond(message, history):
    if message.strip().lower().startswith("wiki:"):
        topic = message.split(":", 1)[1].strip()
        return "üìö ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Wikipedia ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

    if message.strip().lower() == "‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤":
        return awareness.report()

    try:
        result = flow.process(message)
        response = melah.last_spoken if hasattr(melah, 'last_spoken') else "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞"
        speak_voice(response)
        return response
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[Error]: {str(e)}")
        return "‚è≥ ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏• ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞"

# üß† Gradio Interface (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ argument ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ error)
with gr.Blocks(title="Melah Hybrid Agent") as demo:
    gr.Markdown("## üß† Melah Hybrid Agent (Offline GUI)\nAI ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏à ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á")

    gr.ChatInterface(
        fn=respond,
        chatbot=gr.Chatbot(),
        textbox=gr.Textbox(placeholder="‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ wiki: ‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ", container=True)
    )

demo.launch()
‚úÖ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:
‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏°‡∏î‡∏π‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
